    <a id="3410" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3410" class="Generalizable">m</a> <a id="3412" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a>     <a id="3418" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3420" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#186" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
    <a id="3426" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="3428" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a> <a id="3430" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3430" class="Generalizable">U</a>   <a id="3434" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3436" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1059" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="3443" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a>
    <a id="3449" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3449" class="Generalizable">i</a> <a id="3451" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3451" class="Generalizable">j</a> <a id="3453" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3453" class="Generalizable">x</a> <a id="3455" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3455" class="Generalizable">y</a> <a id="3457" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3459" href="Data.Fin.Base.html#1307" class="Datatype">Fin</a> <a id="3463" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a>

</pre>
Extensionally equal subsets are definitionally equal:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="extensionality"></a><a id="3560" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3560" class="Function">extensionality</a> <a id="3575" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="3581" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="3583" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1575" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="3586" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a><a id="3587" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3589" href="Relation.Unary.html#2218" class="Function Operator">≐</a> <a id="3591" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3592" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1575" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="3595" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a><a id="3596" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="3601" class="Symbol">→</a>      <a id="3608" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a>  <a id="3611" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#133" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a>     <a id="3617" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a>
<a id="3619" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3560" class="Function">extensionality</a> <a id="3634" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3636" href="Data.Product.Base.html#2609" class="Function">uncurry</a> <a id="3644" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#6012" class="Function">⊆-antisym</a>
</pre>
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_≟_"></a><a id="3667" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3667" class="Function Operator">_≟_</a> <a id="3671" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3673" href="Relation.Binary.Definitions.html#6217" class="Function">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="3691" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3692" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1059" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="3699" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a><a id="3700" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="3702" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3667" class="Function Operator">_≟_</a> <a id="3706" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3708" href="Data.Vec.Properties.html#1773" class="Function">≡-dec</a> <a id="3714" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#595" class="Function Operator">_≟ᵇ_</a>
</pre>
We define disjointness of sets:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Disjoint"></a><a id="3765" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3765" class="Function">Disjoint</a> <a id="3774" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3776" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1059" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="3783" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a> <a id="3785" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3787" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1059" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="3794" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a> <a id="3796" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3798" href="Agda.Primitive.html#320" class="Primitive">Set</a>
<a id="3802" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3765" class="Function">Disjoint</a> <a id="3811" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3811" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="3813" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3813" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="3815" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3817" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2774" class="Function">Empty</a> <a id="3823" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3824" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3811" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="3826" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2117" class="Function Operator">∩</a> <a id="3828" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3813" class="Bound">T</a><a id="3829" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="Disjoint-as-≡"></a><a id="3832" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3832" class="Function">Disjoint-as-≡</a> <a id="3846" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3848" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3765" class="Function">Disjoint</a> <a id="3857" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="3859" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a> <a id="3861" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3863" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="3865" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2117" class="Function Operator">∩</a> <a id="3867" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a> <a id="3869" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#133" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="3871" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#883" class="Function">∅</a>
<a id="3873" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3832" class="Function">Disjoint-as-≡</a> <a id="3887" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3889" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#3687" class="Function">Empty-unique</a>

    <a id="8486" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="8491" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8492" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8492" class="Bound">y∈⁅x⁆∪S</a> <a id="8500" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#218" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8502" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8502" class="Bound">y≢x</a><a id="8505" class="Symbol">)</a> ← <a id="8509" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8149" class="Function">x∈S-y⇒x∈S×x≢y</a> <a id="8523" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8470" class="Bound">y∈[⁅x⁆∪S]-x</a>
    <a id="8539" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="8544" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#20757" class="Function">x∈p∪q⁻</a> <a id="8551" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8553" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8555" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8492" class="Bound">y∈⁅x⁆∪S</a>
  <a id="8565" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="8570" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="8572" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#675" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="8577" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8577" class="Bound">y∈⁅x⁆</a> <a id="8583" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8585" href="Relation.Nullary.Negation.Core.html#1276" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="8599" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8600" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#5161" class="Function">x∈⁅y⁆⇒x≡y</a> <a id="8610" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8612" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8577" class="Bound">y∈⁅x⁆</a><a id="8617" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8619" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8502" class="Bound">y≢x</a>
  <a id="8625" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="8630" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="8632" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#700" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="8637" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8637" class="Bound">y∈S</a>   <a id="8643" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8645" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#24135" class="Function">x∈p∧x≢y⇒x∈p-y</a> <a id="8659" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8637" class="Bound">y∈S</a> <a id="8663" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8502" class="Bound">y≢x</a>

  <a id="8670" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8670" class="Function">S-x⊆[⁅x⁆∪S]-x</a> <a id="8684" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8686" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8351" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="8688" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2515" class="Function Operator">-</a> <a id="8690" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8353" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8692" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1677" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="8694" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8695" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1356" class="Function Operator">⁅</a> <a id="8697" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8353" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8699" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1356" class="Function Operator">⁆</a> <a id="8701" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2172" class="Function Operator">∪</a> <a id="8703" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8351" class="Bound">S</a><a id="8704" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8706" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2515" class="Function Operator">-</a> <a id="8708" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8353" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="8712" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8670" class="Function">S-x⊆[⁅x⁆∪S]-x</a> <a id="8726" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8726" class="Bound">y∈S-x</a>
    <a id="8736" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="8741" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8742" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8742" class="Bound">x∈S</a> <a id="8746" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#218" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8748" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8748" class="Bound">x≢y</a><a id="8751" class="Symbol">)</a> ← <a id="8755" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8149" class="Function">x∈S-y⇒x∈S×x≢y</a> <a id="8769" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8726" class="Bound">y∈S-x</a>
    <a id="8779" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8781" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#24135" class="Function">x∈p∧x≢y⇒x∈p-y</a> <a id="8795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8796" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#21029" class="Function">x∈p∪q⁺</a> <a id="8803" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8804" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#700" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="8809" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8742" class="Bound">x∈S</a><a id="8812" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="8815" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8748" class="Bound">x≢y</a>

<a id="x∉S⇒S-x≡S"></a><a id="8820" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8820" class="Function">x∉S⇒S-x≡S</a> <a id="8830" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8832" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3453" class="Generalizable">x</a> <a id="8834" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1629" class="Function Operator">∉</a> <a id="8836" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="8838" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8840" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="8842" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2515" class="Function Operator">-</a> <a id="8844" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3453" class="Generalizable">x</a> <a id="8846" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#133" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="8848" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a>
<a id="8850" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8820" class="Function">x∉S⇒S-x≡S</a> <a id="8860" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8861" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="8863" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8865" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8865" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8866" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8868" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8869" class="Argument">S</a> <a id="8871" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8873" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8873" class="Bound">S</a><a id="8874" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8876" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8876" class="Bound">x∉S</a> <a id="8880" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8882" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3560" class="Function">extensionality</a> <a id="8897" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8898" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8923" class="Function">S-x⊆S</a> <a id="8904" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#218" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8906" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8973" class="Function">S⊆S-x</a><a id="8911" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="8915" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="8923" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8923" class="Function">S-x⊆S</a> <a id="8929" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8931" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8873" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="8933" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2515" class="Function Operator">-</a> <a id="8935" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8865" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8937" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1677" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="8939" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8873" class="Bound">S</a>
  <a id="8943" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8923" class="Function">S-x⊆S</a> <a id="8949" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8951" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#2226" class="Field Operator">_₁</a> <a id="8954" href="Function.Base.html#1115" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="8956" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8149" class="Function">x∈S-y⇒x∈S×x≢y</a>

  <a id="8973" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8973" class="Function">S⊆S-x</a> <a id="8979" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8981" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8873" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="8983" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1677" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="8985" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8873" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="8987" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2515" class="Function Operator">-</a> <a id="8989" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8865" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="8993" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8973" class="Function">S⊆S-x</a> <a id="8999" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8999" class="Bound">y∈S</a> <a id="9003" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9005" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#24135" class="Function">x∈p∧x≢y⇒x∈p-y</a> <a id="9019" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8999" class="Bound">y∈S</a> <a id="9023" class="Symbol">λ{</a> <a id="9026" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#190" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="9031" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9033" href="Relation.Nullary.Negation.Core.html#1276" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="9047" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8999" class="Bound">y∈S</a> <a id="9051" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8876" class="Bound">x∉S</a> <a id="9055" class="Symbol">}</a>
</pre>
We define a more ergonomic form of strong induction:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="9124" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="9131" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9131" class="Module">_</a> <a id="9133" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9134" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9136" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9138" href="Relation.Unary.html#1120" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="9143" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9144" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1059" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="9151" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a><a id="9152" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9154" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3390" class="Generalizable">a</a><a id="9155" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="9159" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9160" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9160" class="Bound">P-∅</a> <a id="9164" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9166" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9168" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#883" class="Function">∅</a><a id="9169" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9173" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9174" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9174" class="Bound">P-ind</a> <a id="9180" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9182" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9184" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9185" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9185" class="Bound">S</a><a id="9186" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9188" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9190" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2712" class="Function">Nonempty</a> <a id="9199" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9185" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="9201" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9203" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9204" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1791" class="Function Operator">_⊂</a> <a id="9207" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9185" class="Bound">S</a><a id="9208" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9210" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3360" class="Function Operator">⊆ᴾ</a> <a id="9213" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9215" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9217" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9219" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9185" class="Bound">S</a><a id="9220" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9224" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="9232" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9237" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#2536" class="Module">Wf.All</a> <a id="9244" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9245" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Induction.html#947" class="Function">⊂-wellFounded</a> <a id="9259" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9260" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9151" class="Bound">n</a><a id="9261" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="9264" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="9270" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9271" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#2698" class="Function">wfRec</a><a id="9276" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9280" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9285" href="Relation.Unary.html" class="Module">Relation.Unary</a> <a id="9300" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="9306" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9307" href="Relation.Unary.html#2427" class="Function Operator">_⊆′_</a><a id="9311" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="9316" class="Keyword">private</a>
    <a id="9328" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9328" class="Function">step</a> <a id="9333" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9335" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#803" class="Function">Wf.WfRec</a> <a id="9344" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1791" class="Function Operator">_⊂_</a> <a id="9348" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9350" href="Relation.Unary.html#2427" class="Function Operator">⊆′</a> <a id="9353" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a>
    <a id="9359" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9328" class="Function">step</a> <a id="9364" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9364" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="9366" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9366" class="Bound">P-ind-⊂</a>
      <a id="9380" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="9385" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#3921" class="Function">nonempty?</a> <a id="9395" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9364" class="Bound">S</a>
    <a id="9401" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="9406" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="9408" href="Relation.Nullary.Decidable.Core.html#1659" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a>  <a id="9412" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9412" class="Bound">Empty-S</a> <a id="9420" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="9428" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1707" class="Function">Eq.sym</a> <a id="9435" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9436" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#3687" class="Function">Empty-unique</a> <a id="9449" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9412" class="Bound">Empty-S</a><a id="9456" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9458" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9460" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9160" class="Bound">P-∅</a>
    <a id="9468" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="9473" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="9475" href="Relation.Nullary.Decidable.Core.html#1622" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="9479" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9479" class="Bound">Nonempty-S</a> <a id="9490" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9492" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9174" class="Bound">P-ind</a> <a id="9498" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9479" class="Bound">Nonempty-S</a> <a id="9509" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9510" class="Bound">P-ind-⊂</a> <a id="9518" href="Function.Base.html#2687" class="Function Operator">$-</a><a id="9520" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="9525" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9525" class="Function">strong-induction</a> <a id="9542" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9544" href="Relation.Unary.html#3379" class="Function">Π[</a> <a id="9547" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9549" href="Relation.Unary.html#3379" class="Function">]</a>
  <a id="9553" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9525" class="Function">strong-induction</a> <a id="9570" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9572" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#2698" class="Function">wfRec</a> <a id="9578" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="9580" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="9582" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9328" class="Function">step</a>
</pre>
For convenience, we define a version of strong induction that provides an explicit element of the set:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="9704" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="9711" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9711" class="Module">_</a> <a id="9713" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9714" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9714" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9716" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9718" href="Relation.Unary.html#1120" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="9723" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9724" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1059" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="9731" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a><a id="9732" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9734" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3390" class="Generalizable">a</a><a id="9735" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="9739" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9740" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9740" class="Bound">P-∅</a> <a id="9744" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9746" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9714" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9748" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#883" class="Function">∅</a><a id="9749" class="Symbol">)</a>

We define induction on the elements of a subset:

      <a id="13024" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13024" class="Function">x∉T</a> <a id="13028" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13030" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12396" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13032" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1629" class="Function Operator">∉</a> <a id="13034" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12411" class="Bound">T</a>
      <a id="13042" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13024" class="Function">x∉T</a> <a id="13046" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13048" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#11038" class="Function">Disjoint⁅x⁆⇒x∉</a> <a id="13063" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13064" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#4235" class="Function">Disjoint-∪⁻</a> <a id="13076" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12413" class="Bound">Disjoint-⁅x⁆∪S-T</a><a id="13092" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="13101" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13101" class="Function">Disjoint-S-⁅x⁆∪T</a> <a id="13118" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13120" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3765" class="Function">Disjoint</a> <a id="13129" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12400" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="13131" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13132" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1356" class="Function Operator">⁅</a> <a id="13134" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12396" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13136" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1356" class="Function Operator">⁆</a> <a id="13138" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2172" class="Function Operator">∪</a> <a id="13140" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12411" class="Bound">T</a><a id="13141" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="13149" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13101" class="Function">Disjoint-S-⁅x⁆∪T</a> <a id="13166" class="Symbol">=</a>
        <a id="13176" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#4792" class="Function">Disjoint-swap</a>
          <a id="13200" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13201" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3903" class="Function">Disjoint-sym</a> <a id="13214" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13215" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10884" class="Function">x∉⇒Disjoint⁅x⁆</a> <a id="13230" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12403" class="Bound">x∉S</a><a id="13233" class="Symbol">))</a>
          <a id="13246" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13247" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1803" class="Function">Eq.subst</a> <a id="13256" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13259" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13259" class="Bound">∙</a> <a id="13261" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13263" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3765" class="Function">Disjoint</a> <a id="13272" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13259" class="Bound">∙</a> <a id="13274" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="13277" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13278" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#15507" class="Function">∪-comm</a> <a id="13285" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="13287" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="13290" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12413" class="Bound">Disjoint-⁅x⁆∪S-T</a><a id="13306" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="13311" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13311" class="Function">Disjoint-S-T⇒∣S∪T|≡∣S∣+∣T∣</a> <a id="13338" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13340" href="Relation.Unary.html#3379" class="Function">Π[</a> <a id="13343" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12151" class="Function">P</a> <a id="13345" href="Relation.Unary.html#3379" class="Function">]</a>
  <a id="13349" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13311" class="Function">Disjoint-S-T⇒∣S∪T|≡∣S∣+∣T∣</a> <a id="13376" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13378" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10770" class="Function">induction-on-elements</a> <a id="13400" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12235" class="Function">P-∅</a> <a id="13404" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12307" class="Function">inductive-step</a>
</pre>
We define isomorphisms of finite subsets:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_≅_"></a><a id="13475" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13475" class="Function Operator">_≅_</a> <a id="13479" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13481" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1059" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="13488" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3410" class="Generalizable">m</a> <a id="13490" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13492" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1059" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="13499" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a> <a id="13501" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13503" href="Agda.Primitive.html#320" class="Primitive">Set</a> <a id="13507" class="Symbol">_</a>
<a id="13509" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13509" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="13511" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13475" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="13513" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13513" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="13515" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13517" href="Data.Product.html#657" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13519" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13520" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1575" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13523" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13509" class="Bound">S</a><a id="13524" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13526" href="Function.Bundles.html#9230" class="Function Operator">↔</a> <a id="13528" href="Data.Product.html#657" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13530" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13531" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1575" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13534" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13513" class="Bound">T</a><a id="13535" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
`mk≅` is just a specialized version of `mk↔`, to help with type inference:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="mk≅"></a><a id="13626" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13626" class="Function">mk≅</a> <a id="13630" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13632" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13633" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13633" class="Bound">to</a> <a id="13636" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13638" href="Data.Product.html#657" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13640" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13641" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1575" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13644" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a><a id="13645" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13647" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13649" href="Data.Product.html#657" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13651" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13652" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1575" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13655" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a><a id="13656" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13659" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13660" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13660" class="Bound">from</a> <a id="13665" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13667" href="Data.Product.html#657" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13669" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13670" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1575" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13673" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a><a id="13674" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13676" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13678" href="Data.Product.html#657" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13680" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13681" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1575" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13684" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a><a id="13685" class="Symbol">)}</a>
  <a id="13690" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13692" href="Function.Definitions.html#1224" class="Function">Inverseᵇ</a> <a id="13701" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#133" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a> <a id="13705" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#133" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a> <a id="13709" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13633" class="Bound">to</a> <a id="13712" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13660" class="Bound">from</a>
  <a id="13719" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13721" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="13723" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13475" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="13725" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a>
<a id="13727" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13626" class="Function">mk≅</a> <a id="13731" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13732" class="Argument">to</a> <a id="13735" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13737" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13737" class="Bound">to</a><a id="13739" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13741" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13742" class="Argument">from</a> <a id="13747" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13749" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13749" class="Bound">from</a><a id="13753" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13755" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13757" href="Function.Bundles.html#11069" class="Function">mk↔</a> <a id="13761" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13762" class="Argument">to</a> <a id="13765" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13767" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13737" class="Bound">to</a><a id="13769" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13771" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13772" class="Argument">from</a> <a id="13777" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13779" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13749" class="Bound">from</a><a id="13783" class="Symbol">}</a>
</pre>
<pre class="Agda"><a id="≡-∃∈"></a><a id="13798" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13798" class="Function">≡-∃∈</a> <a id="13803" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13805" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13806" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13806" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13808" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13808" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13810" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13812" href="Data.Product.html#657" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13814" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13815" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1575" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13818" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a><a id="13819" class="Symbol">)}</a>
  <a id="13824" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13826" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13806" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13828" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#2226" class="Field Operator">₁</a> <a id="13830" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#133" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="13832" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13808" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13834" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#2226" class="Field Operator">₁</a>

<a id="S≅∅⇒S≡∅"></a><a id="13886" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13886" class="Function">S≅∅⇒S≡∅</a> <a id="13894" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13896" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="13898" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13475" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="13900" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#883" class="Function">∅</a> <a id="13902" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13903" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a><a id="13904" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13906" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13908" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="13910" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#133" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="13912" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#883" class="Function">∅</a>

<a id="13999" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14006" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14006" class="Module">_</a> <a id="14008" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14009" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14009" class="Bound">S≅T</a> <a id="14013" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14015" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="14017" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13475" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="14019" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a><a id="14020" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14022" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="14030" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14035" href="Function.Bundles.html#6058" class="Module">Inverse</a> <a id="14043" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14009" class="Bound">S≅T</a>

  <a id="14050" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14050" class="Function">to₁-injective</a> <a id="14064" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14066" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14067" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14067" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14069" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14069" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="14071" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14073" href="Data.Product.html#657" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="14075" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14076" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1575" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="14079" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14015" class="Bound">S</a><a id="14080" class="Symbol">)}</a>

    <a id="14204" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14211" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14211" class="Module">_</a> <a id="14213" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14214" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14214" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="14216" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14218" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1059" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="14225" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a><a id="14226" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14228" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14229" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14229" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14230" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14232" class="Keyword">where</a>

      <a id="14278" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14244" class="Function">ι</a> <a id="14280" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14282" href="Data.Product.Base.html#1862" class="Function">map₂</a> <a id="14287" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14288" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#23065" class="Function">p─q⊆p</a> <a id="14294" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="14296" class="Symbol">_)</a>

      <a id="14306" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14306" class="Function">₁∘ι≡₁</a> <a id="14312" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14314" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#2226" class="Field Operator">_₁</a> <a id="14317" href="Function.Base.html#1115" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14319" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14244" class="Function">ι</a> <a id="14321" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1484" class="Function Operator">≗</a> <a id="14323" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#2226" class="Field Operator">_₁</a>
